< Review>
I work nearby and come once a week for lunch to eat and can only speak on their "Siete Mares" soup. At the time of writing this review, I have only come here during the Covid pandemic so have had to order to go and have no experience sitting down and eating at this establishment.

There is ample parking at lunch time in a small plaza. The staff is fairly nice and the interior seems very clean.

Although I can detect a fair amount of flavor boosting seasoning (chicken bouillon), it is extremely tasty.

Can't wait to try the rest of their menu but just can't pull away from this soup.

Highly recommended!<//Review>

< Text>
My coworkers and I ordered from MK today as we are trying to support the local resturants in the area.  We were presently surprised with the quality and freshness of the seafood.and overall ingredients.  We ordered the grilled shrimp burrito, surf and turf quesadilla (which comes with a free shrimp taco only offered on Weds), steak torta, shrimp cocktail, grilled seabass bowl, ceviche mixta tostada and aguachile. Everything was.cooked to perfection..The women that work there take the time to.make sure each dish is prepared perfectly. All the seafood were fresh and not overcooked or dry. Everything was well.ssasoned and not overly salty. My coworker who ordered the shrimp.cocktail could not stop raving about the large juicy shrimp. However she did state that she wished they included more packets of ketchup as she likes her SC with a heavy tomato presence. They give plenty of condiments so you can customize your SC to your preference.<//Text>

< Review>
Heard about this local spot from some friends who swear by the food, so had to give it a try.

This review is based off the brisket burger and service, maybe some of the other menu items are better.

First the service:
There were a few customers already waiting when I placed my order so I expected a bit of a wait, but 35 minutes is more than I would expect for no line and maybe 3 orders before mine.  One of the employees son ordered after me and kept sticking his unmasked face into the interior and talking, regardless of what their opinion of the health crisis is it's terrible to
look like the business doesn't value their customers health.

The food:
The Brisket was cooked perfectly, tender and still juicy, but the marinade had an overpowering flavor of liquid smoke ruining the natural flavor of the meat.  There was sauce on the sandwich when I was told they only put the sauce on the side.

Overall not great especially considering the $15 price, but they do know their way around a smoker.</Review>

<Review>Got inked by Mike Pyro. My first tattoo.   Almost two years ago & still looking sharp. Compared to his more elaborate pieces, with highly detailed shading/lettering, I imagine he could have done mine blinfolded. It was small, simple and only black. It's pretty spacious in here, the tattoo stations were spread out enough as to not feel you're  crowding the other artists and their clients. After speaking  briefly on the phone, he set my appointment for the following day. Immediately,  I felt at ease with him. His energy was cool, calm, confident & I felt honoured to be his canvas. I laid down, lifted my shirt, trying not to move to the rhythm of the punk music and let the art flow, as he leaned into me. Then came the heavy pressure. It was hypnotically  pleasurable and about 30 minutes later,  I felt him pull away from my hip telling me he was done. I felt the pull and didn't want the sensation to end, I wanted more, just a little more ink, please, scribble anything, I wanted to say. He escorted  me out of his station, handing me a business card, confirming I knew about the aftercare for my tattoo. Our hands exchanged the cash, that was that. I was outside under the sun, but still felt him grip my hip, still hearing the buzzing of the needle.</Review>< pictures>

< Review>
I, like I'm sure most of us, we dislike going to the dentist. Even if it's to get ones biannual teeth cleaning or to get a filling for that dreaded cavity.
Whatever type of appointment one might have I will always give a 5 STAR rating to this dental office.
I had an option to get my tooth pulled or to get a root canal, guess which one I chose....??? Yup, I chose the root canal. You'd think that getting your tooth pulled would be less painful but believe you me, getting that shot to numb it all, that's what really hurts.
I swear I made such a big production to avoid it all but the wonderful staff and the great doctor helped me through it all.  I was about to have a panic attack but the staff reassured me that Dr. D was the most wonderful, gentle, and caring doctor they had ever worked with.
Much to my surprise, they were right..!!! Dr. D treated me with such care and was so gentle that I never felt the needle numb my gums.
It's the truth, this is the best dental office I have ever been to and I've made my next appointment for my next procedure.
Thank you 7 Day Dental for making my experience a memorable one. And thank you Dr. D for my bigger smile. 😀</Review>

< review>
I really like the staff at 7 Day Dental.  But the service is not always so good.  Hence the 2 stars.  I think they are good for regular check-ups and cleanings. But anything beyond that, not so much.  The following is my experience.

I came in to repair a tooth that came loose from my upper denture.  The dentist fixed the problem but also recommended I take care of removing the remaining loose teeth that I had.  I agreed and set-up an appointment for the extractions.  The following is a list of the things that surprised and disappointed me from the experience and subsequent follow-ups.

1.	 The extraction dentist had me remove the upper denture, wrapped it in a paper towel and had me hold it.  This is very minor.  But it did strike me as unprofessional.  Every other dentist I’ve been to have cleaned my denture and left it on a tray until the visit was finished.
2.	The dentist was originally going to let me go toothless for 4-6 weeks while my gums heeled from the extractions.  I was super surprised.  I had to ask for a temporary.  It seems like this should have been offered and not requested.
3.	I had to remind the dentist extracting the teeth to take an impression for the temporary denture before removing my remaining teeth.  He protested and said he would do it after the extractions since he had already started numbing my gums.  I questioned him asking if he was sure that would be ok since my gums would be sensitive after the extractions.  I asked that he please talk with the original dentist I spoke to before proceeding.  The dentist stopped him and corrected him, stating that the impressions needed to be taken first.  It was as if they had not consulted with each other on what was to be done.  I would have expected if they had not had a chance to speak, then at a minimum a note would have been left in my file with instructions.
4.	I returned in a few days to get the temporary and was surprised at how off it was from the previous partial denture that was removed.  But then I realized because the dentist did not provide an impression of both the top denture with a mold of the bottom teeth to the lab, they had no reference to match it to.  I didn’t think anything of it at the time the impression was taken.  But when I saw how off the temporary was, then I realized why previous dentists I went to took impressions of both the top and bottom, and sent both to the lab.
5.	Six weeks later now that my mouth has healed I returned for the permanent denture impressions.  I was disappointed to find out that protruding bone should have been filed down during the extractions so that the dentures could fit smoothly.  I was informed that I would have to wait 2 weeks to get approval for the procedure and then wait another 4-6 weeks for my mouth to heal before taking impressions for the dentures.  WHAT!!!!! I couldn’t believe it. Why was this not determined during my original visits??
6.	And today I called to confirm that the request for the latest procedure has been approved.  And was informed that it does not appear that the request was ever submitted.  But they will put in in today.  At this point I am just tired.

Originally I was considering eventually getting implants here.  But after this experience I have decided to still shop around.  At this point I just want to get this procedure finished and be able to eat solid food comfortably.<//review>

I rarely post feedback, but I’ve used 7 Day for two years. Very convenient hours. Especially when I only have time on weekends. Going to other dentists in the past, I always hated going, but I actually enjoy (yes, enjoy) going to 7 Day Dental. I contacted multiple dentist offices to have my wisdom tooth extracted because it was causing me a lot of pain in my upper jaw and making my throat sore. I am on a tight schedule given that I am going abroad to study in less than a week and will not have access to dental care with adequate health insurance. Therefore, I needed to have the extraction as soon as possible. None of the dentists I went to prior to 7-Day Dental could perform the extraction on the same day and charged me an exorbitant amount despite my having Denti-Cal. Fortunately, Dr. Le and Ben at 7-Day Dental were able to perform the extraction on the same day of my first appointment with them. They were very kind to me and the extraction was done quickly and efficiently. I am very grateful to Dr. Le, Ben, the other dental assistants, and the receptionist for their attentiveness and prompt work. < Review>
I am a traveling nurse from Alabama. I felt my tooth break the first day I arrived in Anaheim, California and immediately went into panic mode since I was supposed to start my assignment the next day, and was so far from home. I googled and found this group online and decided to give them a try. I called and made an appointment that night through their emergency hotline and was able to get in first thing at 9 AM the following morning. (Of note, the parking lot and inside of the office/lobby were very clean-a big deal to me being in healthcare)X-rays were taken, and I had a tooth extraction and bone graft placed right there in the office, and it only took 3 hours. Dr. Lisa Tran explained my X-rays and options to me in great detail, and numbed my mouth when it came time for the procedure. Dr. Larry Robinson performed the above mentioned procedure (which was no easy task since my tooth was broken in several places) and sutured the area closed.
